        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/Talk:Title_blacklist" title="Talk:Title blacklist">Title blacklist</a> </td> 
         <td>Propose strings of text that may not be the titles of pages or users on a Wikimedia project. </td>
        </tr>

         <td><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/General_requests" title="Special:MyLanguage/General requests">General requests</a> </td> 
         <td>General requests for Wikimedia improvements, contests, events, collaborations, and services. From important unresolved bugs and feature requests to major new initiatives; a unified summary with pointers to more specific discussions being held elsewhere. </td>
        </tr>

       </tbody>

      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="For_Meta">For Meta</span></h3>

        <tr>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <th style="background:#CCC; text-align:left;" colspan="2">Requests </th>

        </tr>

        <tr> 
         <td><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Meta:Requests_for_help_from_a_sysop_or_bureaucrat" title="Special:MyLanguage/Meta:Requests for help from a sysop or bureaucrat">Help from an admin or bureaucrat</a> </td> 
         <td>Administrators and bureaucrats don't watch every page at all times. Bring up matters that need their attention on this page. </td>
        </tr>

      </table>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="On_other_wikis">On other wikis</span></h2> 
      <p>The tables below list the primary request pages on all wikis that are relevant to Meta request pages such as <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Requests_for_permissions" title="Special:MyLanguage/Requests for permissions">Requests for permissions</a> and <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Requests_for_CheckUser_information" title="Special:MyLanguage/Requests for CheckUser information">Requests for CheckUser information</a>. </p>
      <p>See also the <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/List_of_local_administrator%27s_noticeboards" title="Special:MyLanguage/List of local administrator's noticeboards">List of local administrator's noticeboards</a> for pages where local administrator action against vandalism can be requested. </p>
